    LX.cuts_the_mustard = (function () {
        var enhanced = (
            'addEventListener' in window &&
            'querySelector' in window.document &&
            'localStorage' in window
        );
        return (enhanced || LX.browser.isIE8);
    })();

    LX.cssSupports = function (prop) {
        var div = document.createElement('div'),
            vendors = ['Khtml', 'Ms', 'O', 'Moz', 'Webkit'],
            len = vendors.length;

        if (prop in div.style) {
            return true;
        }

        prop = prop.replace(/^[a-z]/, function (val) {
            return val.toUpperCase();
        });

        while (len--) {
            if (vendors[len] + prop in div.style) {
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    };

    LX.features = {
        supportsAV: !(/(iemobile|windows phone)/).test(navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase()),

        hasTouch: (function () {
            return (('ontouchstart' in window) || window.DocumentTouch && document instanceof DocumentTouch);
        })(),

        fontface: (function () {
            // Exclude if doesn't pass mustard test
            if (!LX.cuts_the_mustard) {
                return false;
            }

            // Exclude false positives
            // http://blog.kaelig.fr/post/33373448491/testing-font-face-support-on-mobile-and-tablet
            if (!!navigator.userAgent.match(/(Android (2.0|2.1))|(Nokia)|(Opera (Mini|Mobi))/)) {
                return false;
            }
            if (!!navigator.userAgent.match(/(w(eb)?OSBrowser)|(UCWEB)|(Windows Phone OS 7)|(XBLWP)|(ZuneWP)/)) {
                return false;
            }

            if (navigator.userAgent.match(/MSIE 10.0/)) return true;

            var style = document.getElementById('font-face-test'),
                sheet = style.sheet || style.styleSheet,
                cssText = '';

            if (sheet) {
                if (sheet.cssRules && sheet.cssRules[0]) {
                    cssText = sheet.cssRules[0].cssText;
                } else {
                    cssText = sheet.cssText || '';
                }
            }

            if (/src/i.test(cssText) && cssText.indexOf('@font-face') === 0) {
                return true;
            }
            return false;
        })(),

        cssAnimations: (function  () {

            // stolen from
            // https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/Guide/CSS/Using_CSS_animations/Detecting_CSS_animation_support
            var animation = false,
                animationstring = 'animation',
                keyframeprefix = '',
                domPrefixes = 'Webkit Moz O ms Khtml'.split(' '),
                pfx  = '',
                elm = document.createElement('div');

            document.documentElement.appendChild(elm);

            if( elm.style.animationName !== undefined ) { animation = true; }

            if( animation === false ) {
                for( var i = 0; i < domPrefixes.length; i++ ) {
                    if( elm.style[ domPrefixes[i] + 'AnimationName' ] !== undefined ) {
                        pfx = domPrefixes[ i ];
                        animationstring = pfx + 'Animation';
                        keyframeprefix = '-' + pfx.toLowerCase() + '-';
                        animation = true;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }

            elm.parentNode.removeChild(elm);

            return animation;
        }()),

        cssSupports: LX.cssSupports,

        svg: (function() {
            return (document.implementation.hasFeature("http://www.w3.org/TR/SVG11/feature#Image", "1.1")) ? true: false;
        }()),

        classList: (function () {
           return (document.documentElement.classList) ? true : false;
        })(),

        cookiesEnabled: (function () {
            var cookiePolicy = window.bbccookies.readPolicy();
            return (
                cookiePolicy.personalisation && cookiePolicy.performance && cookiePolicy.necessary
            );
        })()
    };

    LX.addClass = function (element, cssClass) {
        if (LX.features.classList) {
            element.classList.add(cssClass);
        } else {
            element.className += ' ' + cssClass;
        }
    };

    LX.addFeatureClasses = function () {
        var htmlElement = document.querySelector('html');
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'feature-js');

        if (LX.features.hasTouch) {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'feature-touch');
        } else {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'feature-no-touch');
        }

        if (!LX.features.supportsAV) {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'lx-no-media');
        }

        if (LX.features.fontface) {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'feature-fontface');
        } else {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'feature-no-fontface');
        }

        if (LX.features.svg) {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'svg');
        } else {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'no-svg');
        }

        if (LX.features.cssAnimations) {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'feature-cssanimations');
        }

        if (LX.features.cssSupports('transform')) {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'css-2d-transforms');
        } else {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'no-css-2d-transforms');
        }

        if (LX.cuts_the_mustard) {
            LX.addClass(htmlElement, 'lx-cuts-the-mustard');
        }
    };
    LX.addFeatureClasses();
</script>

  <p><b>West Ham manager Slaven Bilic</b>: "I can explain my feelings, and I can't at the same time. It is great, for me a really great game of football. It was a classic FA Cup tie.   <p><b> Liverpool manager Jurgen Klopp,</b> speaking to BT Sport: "It’s hard. We were the better team, created chances and played good football, but we didn’t use them.</p>
  <p>"There were lots of decisions that on a better day I’d say were funny decisions. I don’t think it was a free-kick [the decision that led to the winning goal] but I’d have to see it again.</p>

morph.init = function() {
    if (!morph.initCalled) {
        morph.markPerformance('morph-init');
        morph.initCalled = true;

        requirejs.config({
            paths: {
                'morph/react'       : '//m.files.bbci.co.uk/releases/1088/vendor/react/react.min',
                'morph/es5-shim'    : '//m.files.bbci.co.uk/releases/1088/vendor/es5-shim/es5-shim.min',
                'morph/es5-sham'    : '//m.files.bbci.co.uk/releases/1088/vendor/es5-shim/es5-sham.min',
                'morph/libs/morph'  : '//m.files.bbci.co.uk/releases/1088/libs/morph/dist/bundle',
                'morph/requirejs'   : '//m.files.bbci.co.uk/releases/1088/vendor/morph-requirejs/index',
                'live-push'         : '//a.files.bbci.co.uk/live-push-handshaker/live/v2/live-push/live-push'
            },
            shim: {
                'morph/react': {
                    deps: ['morph/es5-shim', 'morph/es5-sham']
                },
                'morph/es5-sham': {
                    deps: ['morph/es5-shim']
                }
            }
        });
    }

    requirejs(
        ['morph/react', 'morph/requirejs'],
        function(React) {
            window.React = React;

            requirejs(['morph/libs/morph'], function() {

                if (!morph.runToInits) {
                    morph.markPerformance('morph-init-core-deps-complete');
                    morph.runToInits = true;
                }

                morph.toInit.bundles.forEach(function(bundle) {
                    bundle();
                });
                morph.toInit.bundles = [];
                
                morph.markPerformance('morph-init-bundles-complete');

                morph.toInit.viewModels.forEach(function(viewModel) {
                    viewModel();
                });
                morph.toInit.viewModels = [];

                morph.markPerformance('morph-init-payloads-complete');

                morph.toInit.registers.forEach(function(register) {
                    register();
                });
                morph.toInit.registers = [];

                morph.markPerformance('morph-init-registers-complete');
            });
        }
    );
};
